This file lists every transcription factor binding IGR proposed to regulate an operon, and statistics for the operon composition for each regulatory occurrence of the IGR
If IGR occurrence isn't associated to an operon, it isnt included when calculating statistics
IGR = ClusterID, AVG_OP_LEN = Average number of genes per operon to 3 D.P,TF = Name of TF(s) IGR binds separated by comma, TOTAL_ASSOC = Number of IGR occurrences associated to operon(s), GENE = Name of gene if known, OCC_IN_OPERON = Number of operons associated to IGR bearing gene
IGR	AVG_OP_LEN	TF	TOTAL_ASSOCS	GENE	OCC_IN_OPERON	PERCENT_OPERONS
